         <article itemscope="" itemtype="http://nik.io/v1/schema/Article">
          <span content="2010-10-29 15:37:34" itemprop="lastModifiedDate">
          </span>
          <span content="Safeway Back To School Giveaway" itemprop="title">
          </span>
          <span content="Contest" itemprop="categories">
          </span>
          <span content="Betty Crocker~box tops for education~Dominick~Facebook~safeway~totino" itemprop="tags">
          </span>
          <span content="wordpress.org" itemprop="srcType">
          </span>
          <span content="http://lisacooking.com/2010/08/17/safeway-back-to-school-giveaway/" itemprop="permalink">
          </span>
          <span content="" id="wpLogin" itemprop="wpLogin">
          </span>
          <p>
           <em>
            This giveaway is now over.  The winner is Nicole Greene. Congrats!
           </em>
          </p>
          <p>
           The Safeway family of stores (which includes Dominicks, Tom Thumb, Randalls, Vons, and Genuardis) is making it simple to give back to your local schools with 
           <a href="http://www.2ways2earn.com/" target="_blank">
            2 Ways 2 Earn
           </a>
            cash for your schools with Box Tops for Education and the 10% Goes Back to Schools program. We collect Box Tops for Madisons school, so I know how important these programs are for small schools like ours. However,Box Tops is making it even easier this year with four new brands participating in the program: Progresso Soup, Totinos Pizza, Betty Crocker Cake Mixes and Gold Medal Flour. This year look for the 10% Goes Back to Schools yellow school bus tags on over 2,000 of your favorite items throughout Safeway from August 11th  September 14th. When you purchase participating products with your Club Card, Safeway will give 10% of the purchase price to the local school of your choice! How awesome is that?
          </p>
          <p>
           Heres how it works:
          </p>
          <ul>
           <li>
            Check your receipt from August 11  September 14. The total will be updated each time you shop.
           </li>
           <li>
            Beginning on September 18, a redemption code will be printed at the bottom of your receipt.
           </li>
           <li>
            Visit
            <a href="http://backtoschools.escrip.com/" target="_blank">
             backtoschools.escrip.com
            </a>
            before October 13 to choose your favorite participating local school, then simply enter your redemption code to make your donation.
           </li>
          </ul>
          <p>
           To learn more about Box Tops for Education and Safeways 10% Goes Back to Schools program, visit
           <a href="http://www.2ways2earn.com/" target="_blank">
            www.2ways2earn.com
           </a>
           . And while youre there, dont forget to enter the
           <a href="http://2ways2earn.com/sweepstakes" target="_blank">
            Safeway Bonus Box Tops Sweepstakes
           </a>
           for a chance to win 1,000 Bonus Box Tops for the participating school of your choice! Also, check out Box Tops for Education on Facebook today! Visit
           <a href="http://www.facebook.com/BoxTopsForEducation" target="_blank">
            Box Tops for Education on Facebook
           </a>
           to Like the program and keep up with the latest news from Box Tops.
          </p>
          <p>
           School funding all over the country is being cut, and this is a great way to help your local schools out. Since I am all for education, heres what I have arranged  one lucky reader will get a Box Top Prize Pack! In it, you will find a $25 Safeway gift card (also valid at Dominicks, Tom Thumb, Randalls, Vons, and Genuardis) that you can use to purchase your favorite Box Tops items, in addition to a Bonus Box Tops certificate with a value of 50 Bonus Box Tops! Heres what you need to do:
          </p>
          <p>
           Tell me which
           <a href="http://www.2ways2earn.com/index/products" target="_blank">
            Box Top products
           </a>
           you would spend your $25 gift card on!
          </p>
          <p>
           These will give you one additional entry (for each thing):
          </p>
          <p>
           1. Twitter about this contest.  Please leave me your username so I can verify and you can get an entry every day that you do this (though make sure you leave a comment so I know you did).  If you want, use something like this:
          </p>
          <blockquote>
           <p>
            @blm03 is giving away a Box Top Prize Pack that includes a $25 gift card! Enter here: http://ow.ly/2qV9S
           </p>
          </blockquote>
          <p>
           2. Add this post to social media sites like Stumble, Digg, Kirtsy, Blogging Zoom, Reddit, Propeller, Etc. (1 extra entry per site)
          </p>
          <p>
           3. Like this post on Facebook (There is a like button at the beginning and the end of this post you can use).
          </p>
          <p>
           4. Add this to any forums you belong too. Please give me the URL, so I can verify.
          </p>
          <p>
           Each of these will give you 5 entries:
          </p>
          <p>
           1.  Blog about this on your blog.  Please give me the URL, so I can verify.
           <br/>
           2.  Subscribe to this blog using either
           <a href="http://feeds.feedburner.com/LisaCooking" target="_blank">
            my email or RSS feed
           </a>
           <br/>
           3.  Add my badge to your sidebar:
          </p>
          <p>
           <a href="http://lisacooking.com">
            <img alt="Lisa Cooking" border="0" src="http://i282.photobucket.com/albums/kk258/blm03_photos/125ad.png"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           <textarea cols="30" rows="3">
            <a href="http://lisacooking.com">
             <img alt="Lisa Cooking" border="0" src="http://i282.photobucket.com/albums/kk258/blm03_photos/125ad.png"/>
            </a>
           </textarea>
          </p>
          <p>
           For
           <strong>
            10
           </strong>
           bonus entries:
          </p>
          <p>
           <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003LN0VUC" target="_blank">
            Subscribe to my blog using your Kindle
           </a>
           !
          </p>
          <p>
           Good luck!  This contest will end August 31st, 2010 at 11:59 PM CST.
          </p>
          <p>
           <em>
            The Safeway gift card, Bonus Box Tops certificate, information and giveaway were all given to me from Safeway and General Mills through MyBlogSpark.
           </em>
          </p>
